# Little Hungary Events   #

add_namespace = LH
add_namespace = LHgeneralevents
add_namespace = LHelections

country_event = {	# The M.O.V.E Convention 
	id = LH.1
	title = LH.1.t
	desc = LH.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_communist_congress
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {	# Arrest them!
		name = LH.1.a
		trigger = { 
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_italy_leaning
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = HUN_backed_move_flag
		set_variable = { HUN_move_pp_gain = -0.05 } 
		set_variable = { HUN_move_stability_factor = 0 } 
		set_variable = { HUN_move_drift_defence_factor = 0.1 } 
		set_variable = { HUN_move_command_power_gain = 0.3 } 
		set_variable = { HUN_move_high_command_cost = 0.45 }  
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_move_idea_move_convention_good_tt
		add_command_power = -10
	}
	
	option = {
		name = LH.1.b # We stand with the Rongyos Gárda
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = HUN_italy_leaning
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		add_command_power = -25
		set_country_flag = HUN_backed_rongyos_flag
		set_power_balance = {
			id = HUN_move_garda_bop
			left_side = HUN_move_bop_power
			right_side = HUN_garda_bop_power
		}
		add_power_balance_value = {
			id = HUN_move_garda_bop 
			value = -0.5
		}
		#add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = HUN_move_dynamic_modifier }
		set_variable = { HUN_move_surrender_limit = 0.5 } #+0.3
		set_variable = { HUN_move_drift_defence_factor = 0.5 } #+0.8
		set_variable = { HUN_move_stability_factor = -0.3 } #-0.2
		set_variable = { HUN_move_high_command_cost = 0.4 } #+0.4
		set_variable = { HUN_move_pp_cost = 0.4 } #+0.4
		set_variable = { HUN_move_army_attack_factor = -0.4 } #-0.4
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_move_idea_move_convention_tt
		
		
	}
}

#Event for Dockyards and Ports in Adriatic
country_event = {
	id = LH.2
	title = LH.2.t
	desc = LH.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_naval_treaty
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		AND = {
			YUG = { 
				has_capitulated = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = LH.2.a
		
		HUN = {
			transfer_state = 45
			transfer_state = 109
			transfer_state = 974
			transfer_state = 971
			transfer_state = 764
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { ITA = { is_in_faction_with = HUN } }
			ITA = {
				transfer_state = 103
				transfer_state = 104
				transfer_state = 105
				transfer_state = 804
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { AUS = { is_in_faction_with = HUN } }
			AUS = {
				transfer_state = 102
				transfer_state = 853
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { BUL = { is_in_faction_with = HUN } }
			BUL = {
				release_puppet = SER
				
				transfer_state = 106
				add_state_core = 106
				transfer_state = 803
				add_state_core = 803
				
				#transfer_state = 802
				#transfer_state = 107
				#transfer_state = 108
				
			}
			
		}
		
		974 = {
			
			add_building_construction = {
				type = dockyard
				level = 2
				instant_build = yes
			}
			
			add_building_construction = {
				type = naval_base
				level = 5
				province = 11564
				instant_build = yes
			}								
		}
		
		163 = {
				
			add_building_construction = {
				type = dockyard
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			
			add_building_construction = {
				type = naval_base
				level = 2
				province = 3943
				instant_build = yes
			}								
		}
		736 = {
				
			add_building_construction = {
				type = dockyard
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			
			add_building_construction = {
				type = naval_base
				level = 2 
				province = 6626
				instant_build = yes
			}								
		}
		157 = {
				
			add_building_construction = {
				type = dockyard
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			
			add_building_construction = {
				type = naval_base
				level = 2
				province = 925
				instant_build = yes
			}								
		}
	}
}

# Ask Germany for Sudetenland and Czech Lands
country_event = {
	id = LH.3 
	title = LH.3.t
	desc = LH.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_naval_treaty
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	#Demand the Territory
	option = {
		name = LH.3.a 
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				is_in_faction_with = HUN
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		GER = {country_event = LH.4}
	}
	
	#No thanks
	option = {
		name = LH.3.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
	}
	
}

# Germanys Response
country_event = {
	id = LH.4
	title = LH.4.t
	desc = LH.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_naval_treaty

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	#mean_time_to_happen = {
	#	days = 20
	#}
	
	#Sure
	option = {
		name = LH.4.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				strength_ratio = { tag = AUS ratio < 0.8 }
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				69 = {
					is_owned_by = GER
				}
			}
			AUS = { transfer_state = 69 }
			AUS = {
				add_state_core = 69
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				9 = {
					is_owned_by = GER
				}
			}
			AUS = { transfer_state = 9 }
			AUS = {
				add_state_core = 9
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				74 = {
					is_owned_by = GER
				}
			}
			AUS = { transfer_state = 74 }
			AUS = {
				add_state_core = 74
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				75 = {
					is_owned_by = GER
				}
			}
			AUS = { transfer_state = 75 }
			AUS = {
				add_state_core = 75
			}
		}
		GER = {
			remove_state_core  = 69
			remove_state_claim = 69
			remove_state_core  = 9
			remove_state_core  = 74
			remove_state_core  = 75
			
		}
		
	}
	#No way
	option = {
		name = LH.4.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
			modifier = { 
				strength_ratio = { tag = AUS ratio > 1.25 } #stronger than Austria
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = { 
				strength_ratio = { tag = ITA ratio > 1.25 } #stronger than Italy
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = { 
				strength_ratio = { tag = HUN ratio > 1.25 } #stronger than Hungary
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		AUS = {country_event = LH.5}
	}
}

# Germany refused
country_event = {
	id = LH.5
	title = LH.5.t
	desc = LH.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_naval_treaty
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#mean_time_to_happen = {
	#	days = 20
	#}
	
	#Then war
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				is_in_faction_with = HUN
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		name = LH.5.a
		AUS = {
			add_state_core = 9
			add_state_core = 69
			add_state_core = 74
			add_state_core = 75
		}
		create_wargoal = {
				type = take_state_focus
				target = GER
				generator = { 69 9 74 75}
			}
	}
	
	#Okay
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		name = LH.5.b
		add_stability = -0.1
	}
}

	id = LH.13
	title = LH.13.t
	desc = LH.13.desc 
	picture = GFX_report_event_hungary_parliament
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {# fold
		name = LH.13.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				is_in_faction = no
				HUN = { is_in_faction = yes }
				factor = 3
			}
			modifier = {
				strength_ratio = { tag = HUN ratio < 1 }
				factor = 4
			}
		}
		HUN = { country_event = LH.14 }
	}
	option = {# refuse
		name = LH.13.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 70
			modifier = {
				has_stability < 0.5
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		HUN = { country_event = LH.15 }
		 
	}
}

#Demand Croatia event chain - Yugoslavia folds
country_event = {
	id = LH.14
	title = LH.14.t
	desc = LH.14.desc 
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_peaceful_annexation
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {# great
		name = LH.14.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = HUN_claim_croatia
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				YUG = { 
					release = CRO 
				}
			}
			puppet = CRO
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					YUG = {
						has_full_control_of_state = 974
					}
				}
				HUN = {
					transfer_state = 974
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					YUG = {
						has_full_control_of_state = 109
					}
				}
				HUN = {
					transfer_state = 109
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					YUG = {
						has_full_control_of_state = 103
					}
				}
				HUN = {
					transfer_state = 103
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = CRO
					CRO = {
						has_full_control_of_state = 109
					}
				}
				HUN = {
					transfer_state = 109
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = CRO
					CRO = {
						has_full_control_of_state = 971
					}
				}
				HUN = {
					transfer_state = 971
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = CRO
					CRO = {
						has_full_control_of_state = 103
					}
				}
				HUN = {
					transfer_state = 103
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = CRO
					CRO = {
						has_full_control_of_state = 102
					}
				}
				HUN = {
					transfer_state = 102
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Demand Vojvodina event chain - Yugoslavia refuses
country_event = {
	id = LH.15
	title = LH.15.t
	desc = LH.15.desc 
	picture = GFX_report_event_hungary_refused
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {# back down
		name = LH.15.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				has_war = yes
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05

	}
	
	option = {# Go alone
		name = LH.15.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				AND = {
					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ITA }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_wargoal_against = YUG }
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = take_state_focus
				target = YUG
				generator = { 109 970 103 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = news.308 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = LH.17
	title = LH.17.t
	desc = {
		text = LH.17.no_focus.d
		trigger = {	
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_germany_leaning
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_italy_leaning
			}
			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = HUN_continue_bethlens_consolidation
			}
			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = HUN_social_reforms
			}
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		text = LH.17.consolidation.d
		trigger = {	
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_germany_leaning
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_italy_leaning
			}
			
			has_completed_focus = HUN_continue_bethlens_consolidation
			
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		text = LH.17.ger_leaning.d
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = HUN_germany_leaning
		}
	}
	
	desc = {

		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = HUN_italy_leaning
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		text = LH.17.march_front.d 
		trigger = {	
			AND = {
				has_completed_focus = HUN_social_reforms 
				has_country_flag = HUN_democratic_path_chosen
			}
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		text = LH.17.communist.d

			AND = {
				has_completed_focus = HUN_social_reforms 
				has_country_flag = HUN_communist_path_chosen_flag
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = HUN_rescue_bela_kun
					has_completed_focus = HUN_grant_general_amnesty
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		text = LH.17.kun.d 
		trigger = {	
			has_completed_focus = HUN_rescue_bela_kun
		}
	}

			has_completed_focus = HUN_grant_general_amnesty
		}
	}

		days = 1
	}

		set_country_flag = new_prime_minister_36
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = HUN_rescue_bela_kun
					}
				}
				retire_character = HUN_gyula_gombos_de_jakfa
			}
			
		}
	}

	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = HUN
	}
	
	option = { # a fascist Prime Minister
		name = LH.17.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = HUN_continue_bethlens_consolidation
					has_completed_focus = HUN_empower_the_far_right
					has_completed_focus = HUN_social_reforms
				}
				has_country_flag = HUN_germany_leaning
				has_country_flag = HUN_italy_leaning
			}
		}
		HUN = {
			country_event = { id = LH.118 hours = 6 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { # a conservative prime minister
		name = LH.17.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = HUN_continue_bethlens_consolidation
					has_completed_focus = HUN_empower_the_far_right
					has_completed_focus = HUN_social_reforms
				}
				has_completed_focus = HUN_continue_bethlens_consolidation
				
			}
		}
		HUN = {
			country_event = { id = LH.119 hours = 6 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { # a socialist prime minister
		name = LH.17.c
		trigger = {

					has_completed_focus = HUN_empower_the_far_right

				}

					has_completed_focus = HUN_social_reforms

		}

	}

		name = LH.118.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = HUN_continue_bethlens_consolidation
					has_completed_focus = HUN_empower_the_far_right
					has_completed_focus = HUN_social_reforms
				}
				has_country_flag = HUN_germany_leaning
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			deactivate_advisor = HUN_bela_imredy
		}
		activate_advisor = HUN_bela_imredy_prime
		set_country_flag = HUN_imredy_prime_flag
		if = {
			limit = { OR = { has_completed_focus = HUN_a_new_middle_class NOT = { has_completed_focus = HUN_strengthen_the_regency } } }
			promote_character = HUN_bela_imredy
		}
	}
	
	option = {# We need Szálasi
		name = LH.118.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = HUN_continue_bethlens_consolidation
					has_completed_focus = HUN_empower_the_far_right
					has_completed_focus = HUN_social_reforms
				}
				has_country_flag = HUN_germany_leaning
			}
			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = HUN_strengthen_the_regency
			}
		}		
		
		hidden_effect = { deactivate_advisor = HUN_szalasi_ferenc }
		activate_advisor = HUN_szalasi_ferenc_prime
		set_country_flag = HUN_szalasi_prime_flag
		
		
		
		## Change Advisors to right trait ##
		
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_trait = {
				character = HUN_ferenc_rajniss
				slot = political_advisor
				trait = editor
			}
			add_trait = {
				character = HUN_ferenc_rajniss
				slot = political_advisor
				trait = minister_of_education
			}
		}
			
	}
	
	option = {# We will call the Rongyos Gárda
		name = LH.118.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = HUN_continue_bethlens_consolidation
					has_completed_focus = HUN_empower_the_far_right

		remove_advisor_role = {
			character = "HUN_szalasi_ferenc"

		}
		
	}
	
	option = {# We don't need a prime minister haha

		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_no_prime_minister_tt

		add_political_power = 70
	}
	
}

#Event for empower the right, choose germany or italy
country_event = {
	id = LH.19
	title = LH.19.t
	desc = {
		text = LH.19.not_chosen_prime.d
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_gombos_alive
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = gombos_death
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = LH.19.chosen_ger_prime.d
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_imredy_prime_flag
				has_country_flag = HUN_szalasi_ferenc_prime
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = LH.19.chosen_ita_prime.d
		trigger = {
			has_idea = HUN_ivan_hejjas
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	#mean_time_to_happen = {
	#	days = 1
	#}
	
	
	option = {# turn to germany
		name = LH.19.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_imredy_prime_flag
				has_country_flag = HUN_szalasi_prime_flag
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = HUN_gombos_alive
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = gombos_death
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = HUN_germany_leaning
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = HUN_GER_diplomacy }
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = HUN modifier = HUN_GER_diplomacy }
		HUN_add_10_influence_points = yes 
		HUN_substract_10_agitation = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_allow_szalasi_imredy_tt
	}
	
	
	option = {# turn to italy
		name = LH.19.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = HUN_ivan_hejjas
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = HUN_gombos_alive
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = gombos_death
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = HUN_italy_leaning
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = ITA modifier = HUN_ITA_diplomacy }
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = ITA modifier = HUN_ITA_diplomacy }
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_allow_hejjas_tt
	}

					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = HUN_carpathian_coup_flag
				}
				
			}
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		text = LH.22.not_fascist.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = HUN_empower_the_far_right
			}
		}
	
	}
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_speech
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = HUN				
		AND = {
			GER = {
			has_completed_focus = GER_end_of_czechoslovakia
			}
			NOT = {
				ROOT = {
					has_country_flag = HUN_slovakia_overlordship_claimed_flag
					has_completed_focus = HUN_accept_the_habsburg_prince
				}
				
			}
			has_full_control_of_state = 73
		}		
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 20
	}

	
	immediate = { 
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					GER =  { check_variable = { var = ger_alignment_influence value = 60 compare = less_than_or_equals } }
					HUN = { has_full_control_of_state = 71 }
				}
				
				
			}
			GER = { add_to_variable = { var = ger_alignment_influence value = 40 } }
		}
		
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					GER =  { check_variable = { var = ger_alignment_influence value = 80 compare = less_than_or_equals } }
					NOT = {
						HUN = { has_full_control_of_state = 71 }
					}
					HUN = { has_full_control_of_state = 73 }
				}
			}
			GER = { add_to_variable = { var = ger_alignment_influence value = 20 } }
		}
		
	}

				has_government = fascism

country_event = {
	id = LH.26
	title = LH.26.t
	desc = LH.26.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_politician_speech
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = HUN	
		has_government = neutrality
		NOT = {
			ROOT = {
				OR = {
					has_completed_focus = HUN_empower_the_far_right
					has_completed_focus = HUN_arrow_cross_deal
				}
			}
		}
		GER =  { check_variable = { var = ger_alignment_influence value = 85 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		HUN = { is_in_faction = no }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 20
	}

	
	immediate = { 
		set_country_flag = HUN_german_ultimatum_received
	}

	option = {# We have no choice...
		name = LH.26.a
		GER = {
			add_to_faction = HUN
		}
	}
	
	option = {# No, we will not accept this fate!
		name = LH.26.b
		kill_country_leader = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_istvan_succ}
			promote_character = HUN_istvan_horthy
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_otto_succ}
			HUN_otto_von_habsburg = {
				promote_character = {
					Ideology = despotism
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_albrecht_succ}
			HUN_albrecht_habsburg = {
				promote_character = {
					Ideology = despotism
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = {has_country_flag = HUN_found_succession}}
			promote_character = HUN_regency_council
		}
				
		hidden_effect = {			
			GER = {country_event = { id = LH_GER.1 days = 7 }}
		}
	}
	
}

#1939 elections
country_event = {
	id = LH.29
	title = LH.29.t
	desc = LH.29.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_gathering_protest
	
	is_triggered_only = no
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	
	immediate = { 
		set_variable = { var = nep_pop value = party_popularity@neutrality }
		set_variable = { var = szdp_pop value = party_popularity@democratic }
		set_variable = { var = nap_pop value = party_popularity@fascism }
	}
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = HUN
		date > 1939.05.24
		has_government = neutrality
		OR = {
			has_completed_focus = HUN_strengthen_the_regency
			has_completed_focus = HUN_strengthen_the_regency_monarch
			has_completed_focus = HUN_call_for_a_revisionist_king
		} 
		HUN = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_completed_focus = HUN_accept_the_habsburg_prince
				}
			}
		}
		
		
	}

	option = {# The People have spoken
		name = LH.29.a
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_elections_39_tt
		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = HUN_strengthen_the_regency_monarch } has_country_flag = HUN_historical_activated_flag } 
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { var = nap_pop value = 0.25 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				add_ideas = HUN_divided_nation
				set_country_flag = HUN_elections_divided_nation_flag
			}	
		
			#hidden_effect = {
				add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = szdp_pop}
				add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.15}
				
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 3
				}
				set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality name = HUN_MEP long_name = HUN_MEP_long }
				set_party_name = { ideology = fascism long_name = HUN_nyilas_party_long name = HUN_nyilas_party }
				set_party_name = { ideology = democratic long_name = HUN_szdp_party_long name = HUN_szdp_party }
			#}
		}
		else = {
			set_political_party = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 70
			}
			set_political_party = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = 4
			}
			set_political_party = {
				ideology = fascism 
				popularity = 26
			}
		}
	}	
}

		name = LH.33.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = { target = HUN value < 25} 
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				political_power_daily < 1
				factor = 3
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories < 30
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = { target = HUN value < 40} 
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				if = {
					limit = { 
						ROOT = {
							has_government = democratic
						}
					}
					HUN = { 
						OR = {
							has_completed_focus = HUN_renounce_trianon 
							has_completed_focus = HUN_renounce_trianon_monarch
						}
					}
				}
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							NOT = {
								has_government = fascism
							}
						}
					}
					GER =  { 
						AND = {
							check_variable = { var = ger_alignment_influence value = 15 compare = greater_than_or_equals } 
							check_variable = { var = ger_alignment_influence value = 25 compare = less_than } 
						}
					}
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							NOT = {
								has_government = fascism
							}
						}
					}
					GER =  { 
						AND = {
							check_variable = { var = ger_alignment_influence value = 25 compare = greater_than_or_equals } 
							check_variable = { var = ger_alignment_influence value = 35 compare = less_than } 
						}
					}
				}
				factor = 3
			}
			modifier = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							NOT = {
								has_government = fascism
							}
						}
					}
					GER =  { 
						AND = {
							check_variable = { var = ger_alignment_influence value = 35 compare = greater_than_or_equals } 
							check_variable = { var = ger_alignment_influence value = 45 compare = less_than } 
						}
					}
				}
				factor = 4
			}
			modifier = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							NOT = {
								has_government = fascism
							}
						}
					}
					GER =  { 
						AND = {
							check_variable = { var = ger_alignment_influence value = 50 compare = greater_than_or_equals }  
						}
					}
				}
				factor = 5
			}
		}

#Country accepts economic help
country_event = {
	id = LH.35
	title = LH.35.t
	desc = LH.35.d 
	
	fire_only_once = no
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_french_liberation
	
	
	option = {# great!
		name = LH.35.a
		set_country_flag = {
			flag = HUN_trade_recently_upgraded
			days = 120
			value = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = HUN_blockaded_economy }
			remove_ideas = HUN_blockaded_economy
		}
		hidden_effect = { ### If you're just switching between partners
			if = {
				limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = HUN_trade_deal_modifier } }
				set_country_flag = HUN_already_trade_flag
				HUN_reset_trade_deal_modifier = yes
				if = {
					limit = { 
						FROM = { 
							NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
							NOT = { tag = GER }
						}
					}
					HUN_add_10_agitation = yes
				}
				else = {
					HUN_substract_10_agitation = yes
					HUN_add_10_influence_points = yes
				}
			}	
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = HUN_trade_deal_modifier } 
		}
		clr_country_flag = HUN_no_trade_partner_flag 		
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = ENG } }
			HUN_set_trade_deal_eng = yes
			HUN_add_10_agitation = yes		
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = FRA } }
			HUN_set_trade_deal_fra = yes
			HUN_add_10_agitation = yes				
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = SOV } } 
			HUN_set_trade_deal_sov = yes 		
			HUN_add_10_agitation = yes	
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = GER } }
			HUN_set_trade_deal_ger = yes
			HUN_substract_10_agitation = yes
			HUN_add_10_influence_points = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = ITA } }
			HUN_set_trade_deal_ita = yes
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { ITA = { is_in_faction_with = GER } } }
				HUN_add_10_agitation = yes	
			}
			else = {
				HUN_add_10_influence_points = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = USA } }
			HUN_set_trade_deal_usa = yes
			HUN_add_10_agitation = yes					
		}
		
		### MODIFY ECONOMIC CRISIS ###
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_modify_crisis_each_month_tt 
		HUN_modify_crisis_all_tt = yes 
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_economic_crisis_1_consumer_goods
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_economic_crisis_2_construction_speed
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_economic_crisis_2_factory_output
	}

}

#(Hidden?) Event that slowly increases the Economic Crisis until a specific level
country_event = {
	id = LH.37
	title = LH.37.t
	desc = LH.37.d 
	
	fire_only_once = no
	
	is_triggered_only = no 
	
	trigger = {
		has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = HUN_trade_deal_modifier }
		has_country_flag = HUN_trade_deal_accepted_flag
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = HUN_trade_upgrade_flag
				value < 6
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_trade_upgrade_flag }
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_cancel_trade_flag }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_trade_recently_upgraded }
		HUN_dynamic_modifier_remove_trigger = no
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 40 }
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_crowd_in_prague
	
	immediate = {
		
	}
	
	option = {# great!
		name = LH.37.a
		HUN_add_1_consumer = yes
		HUN_add_2_construction = yes
		HUN_add_2_factory_output = yes
		
		HUN_set_consumer_trade_deal = yes
		HUN_set_construction_trade_deal = yes
		HUN_set_output_trade_deal = yes
		
		set_country_flag = {
			flag = HUN_trade_recently_upgraded
			days = 120
			value = 1
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_trade_upgrade_flag } }
			set_country_flag = {
				flag = HUN_trade_upgrade_flag
				value = 1
			}
		}
		else = {
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = HUN_trade_upgrade_flag
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

#Event to remove the Trade Deal if no Trade route found due to war or whatever
country_event = {
	id = LH.38
	title = LH.38.t
	desc = LH.38.d 
	
	fire_only_once = no
	
	is_triggered_only = no 
	
	trigger = {
		HUN_dynamic_modifier_remove_trigger = yes
		has_country_flag = HUN_trade_deal_accepted_flag
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_stock_traders

	option = {# shit 
		name = LH.38.a
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = HUN_trade_deal_modifier }
		clr_country_flag = HUN_already_trade_flag
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = {
					flag = HUN_trade_deal_accepted_flag
					days < 1270
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_loose_bonuses_war_tt
			HUN_remove_trade_deal_bonuses = yes
		}
		HUN_reset_trade_deal_modifier = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				HUN_has_economic_crisis = yes
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = HUN_blockaded_economy
				days = 200
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_usa_trade_partner_flag
			}
			USA = { remove_ideas = HUN_giving_economic_help }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_eng_trade_partner_flag
			}
			ENG = { remove_ideas = HUN_giving_economic_help }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_ita_trade_partner_flag
			}
			ITA = { remove_ideas = HUN_giving_economic_help }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_ger_trade_partner_flag
			}
			GER = { remove_ideas = HUN_giving_economic_help }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_fra_trade_partner_flag
			}
			FRA = { remove_ideas = HUN_giving_economic_help }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_sov_trade_partner_flag
			}
			SOV = { remove_ideas = HUN_giving_economic_help }
		}
		add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = -3 }
	}
}

#FIRST EVENT AFTER INDUSTRIAL REV FOR SPECIAL FACTORY SORG RT
country_event = {	
	id = LH.36
	title = LH.36.t
	desc = LH.36.d 
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = no
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_special_construction_cooldown_flag }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_special_factory_construction_flag }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_sorg_completed_flag }
		has_completed_focus = HUN_industrial_rev
		HUN_has_economic_crisis = yes
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 44 }
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_factory
	
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = {
			flag = HUN_special_construction_cooldown_flag
			days = 145
			value = 1
		}
	}

	option = {# invest
		name = LH.36.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_start_construction_special_factory_tt
		activate_decision = HUN_construct_sorg_factory
		set_country_flag = HUN_special_factory_construction_flag
	}
	
	option = {# Forget it
		name = LH.36.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_project_never_again_tt
		set_country_flag = HUN_sorg_completed_flag
	}
	
	option = {# Later
		name = LH.36.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_project_for_later_tt
	}
}

		}

		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				YUG = {
					has_idea = YUG_idea_croatian_opposition
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = YUG_idea_croatian_opposition
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				YUG = {
					has_idea = YUG_idea_croats_suppressed
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = YUG_idea_croats_suppressed
		}

		#		set_nationality = HUN
		#	}
		#}

# Austrian Referendum - event for Austria to allow it
country_event = {
	id = LH.109
	title = LH.109.t
	desc = LH.109.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #sure
		name = LH.109.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80

		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { HUN = { has_completed_focus = HUN_reintegrate_railroads } }
					NOT = { AUS = { has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 75 } } }
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				70 = { AUS = { country_event = { id = LH.110 hours = 24 } } } #country votes yes
				30 = { AUS = { country_event = { id = LH.111 hours = 24 } } } #country votes no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						HUN = { has_completed_focus = HUN_reintegrate_railroads } 
						NOT = { AUS = { has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 75 } } }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { HUN = { has_completed_focus = HUN_reintegrate_railroads } }
						AUS = { has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 75 } } 
					}
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				80 = { AUS = { country_event = { id = LH.110 hours = 24 } } } #country votes yes
				20 = { AUS = { country_event = { id = LH.111 hours = 24 } } } #country votes no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					HUN = { has_completed_focus = HUN_reintegrate_railroads } 
					AUS = { has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 75 } } 
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				95 = { AUS = { country_event = { id = LH.110 hours = 24 } } } #country votes yes
				5 = { AUS = { country_event = { id = LH.111 hours = 24 } } } #country votes no
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #no
		name = LH.109.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				has_government = democratic
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		HUN = { country_event = { id = LH.114 hours = 6 } }
	}

	option = { #sure, but we'll make sure it gets the right result
		name = LH.109.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 160 }
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = communism
				has_government = fascism
			}
		}
		add_threat = -2
		add_political_power = -50
		AUS = { country_event = { id = LH.115 hours = 24 } }
		set_global_flag = HUN_referendum_shenanigans
	}
}

				}

				create_country_leader = {

					desc = "POLITICS_FRIEDRICH_FRANZ_OF_MECKLENBURG-SCHWERIN_DESC"

						fascist_sympathies
					}

				}
				hidden_effect = {
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Friedrich Franz of Mecklenburg-Schwerin"
						desc = "POLITICS_FRIEDRICH_FRANZ_OF_MECKLENBURG-SCHWERIN_DESC"
						picture = GFX_Portrait_hungary_friedrich_franz
						expire = "1965.1.1"

						traits = {
						}

					}
				}
				else = {
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Friedrich Franz of Mecklenburg-Schwerin"
						desc = "POLITICS_FRIEDRICH_FRANZ_OF_MECKLENBURG-SCHWERIN_DESC"
						picture = GFX_Portrait_hungary_friedrich_franz
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = nazism
						traits = {
						}
						id = 502 #Nazi Franz
					}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
				news_event = { id = news.297 }
				
				
			}
	}

		name = LH.122.b
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.05 }
			HUN_albrecht_habsburg = {
				promote_character = {
					Ideology = despotism
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				HUN_albrecht_habsburg = {
					promote_character = {
						Ideology = gen_nazism
					}
				}

country_event = {	# annex aus after capitulating them
	id = LH.129
	title = LH.129.t
	desc = LH.129.d 
	picture = GFX_report_event_three_kingdoms
	
	is_triggered_only = no
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_completed_focus = HUN_formalize_treaty
		has_global_flag = HUN_AUS_refused_flag
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = HUN_traditional_model_flag
			has_country_flag = HUN_democratic_model_flag
		}
		has_full_control_of_state = 978
		has_full_control_of_state = 4
		has_full_control_of_state = 153
		has_full_control_of_state = 152
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7
	}
	
	option = { #Yes
		name = LH.129.a
		#add_state_core = 978
		#add_state_core = 4
		#add_state_core = 152
		#add_state_core = 153
		
		### HMS Government ### (Puppet the countries)
		
		if = {
			limit = { 
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_completed_focus = HUN_hms_responsible_government
						NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_traditional_model_flag }
					}
					has_country_flag = HUN_confederation_democracy_flag
				}
			}
			release_puppet = AUS
			set_autonomy = { target = AUS autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet }
			AUS = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = AUS_DEMOCRATIC_MONARCHY
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_joseph_chosen_flag }
				AUS = {
					add_ideas = HUN_joseph_idea_other_nations
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_otto_chosen_flag }
				AUS = {
					add_ideas = HUN_otto_idea_other_nations
				}
			}
		}
		
		### Danubian Confederation ### (Annex the countries)
		
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_global_flag = HUN_CZE_agreed_flag
				OR = {	
					has_completed_focus = HUN_habsburg_middle
					AND = {
						has_completed_focus = HUN_hms_responsible_government
						has_country_flag = HUN_traditional_model_flag
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = HUN_confederation_democracy_flag
				}
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = HUN_PREEMPIRE
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = HUN_annexed_czech_flag
				OR = {	
					has_completed_focus = HUN_habsburg_middle
					AND = {
						has_completed_focus = HUN_hms_responsible_government
						has_country_flag = HUN_traditional_model_flag
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = HUN_confederation_democracy_flag
				}
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = HUN_PREEMPIRE
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_global_flag = HUN_CZE_refused_flag 
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = HUN_annexed_czech_flag
					has_country_flag = HUN_confederation_democracy_flag
				}
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = HUN_AUS
			set_country_flag = HUN_annexed_austria_flag
		}
		
	}

}

				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { has_government = communism }
				has_civil_war = no
				has_completed_focus = SPA_settle_the_succession_question
			}
		}
		
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = SPR
				NOT = { has_government = communism }
			}
			country_event = {
				id = LH.139
				days = 7
			}
			hidden_effect = { save_global_event_target_as = hungary_wedding_partner }
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Portugal Infanta Maria Adelaide
		name = LH.137.b
		trigger = {
			any_other_country = {
				original_tag = POR
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { has_government = communism }
				#has_completed_focus = SPA_settle_the_succession_question
			}
		}
		
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = POR
				NOT = { has_government = communism }
			}
			country_event = {
				id = LH.139
				days = 7
			}
			hidden_effect = { save_global_event_target_as = hungary_wedding_partner }
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Maybe we should reconsider...
		name = LH.137.c
		country_event = LH.135
	}

country_event = { # Second Revision: Burgenland and Southern Slovakia
	id = LH.152
	title = LH.152.t 
	desc = LH.152.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hun_parade
	
	is_triggered_only = no
	
	fire_only_once = yes 
	
	trigger = {
		has_full_control_of_state = 664
		has_full_control_of_state = 978
		OR = {
			has_idea = HUN_first_revision_b
			has_idea = HUN_first_revision_ss
			has_idea = HUN_first_revision_v
			has_idea = HUN_first_revision_nt
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	option = { # 
		name = LH.152.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = HUN_first_revision_b }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = HUN_first_revision_b
				add_idea = HUN_second_revision_b_ss
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = HUN_first_revision_ss }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = HUN_first_revision_ss
				add_idea = HUN_second_revision_b_ss
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = HUN_first_revision_v }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = HUN_first_revision_v
				add_idea = HUN_second_revision_b_ss
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = HUN_first_revision_nt }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = HUN_first_revision_nt
				add_idea = HUN_second_revision_b_ss
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				NOT = { 
					664 = { 
						is_core_of = HUN 
					} 
					has_country_flag = HUN_ss_evacuated_flag
				}
			}
			add_state_core = 664
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				NOT = { 
					978 = { 
						is_core_of = HUN 
					} 
				}
			}
			add_state_core = 978
		}
		
	}
}

	fire_only_once = yes 
	
	trigger = {
		has_full_control_of_state = 664
		has_full_control_of_state = 45
		OR = {
			has_idea = HUN_first_revision_b
			has_idea = HUN_first_revision_ss
			has_idea = HUN_first_revision_v
			has_idea = HUN_first_revision_nt
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	option = { # 
		name = LH.155.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = HUN_first_revision_b }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = HUN_first_revision_b
				add_idea = HUN_second_revision_ss_v
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = HUN_first_revision_ss }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = HUN_first_revision_ss
				add_idea = HUN_second_revision_ss_v
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = HUN_first_revision_v }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = HUN_first_revision_v
				add_idea = HUN_second_revision_ss_v
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = HUN_first_revision_nt }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = HUN_first_revision_nt
				add_idea = HUN_second_revision_ss_v
			}
		}
		
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				NOT = { 
					664 = { 
						is_core_of = HUN 
					} 
					has_country_flag = HUN_ss_evacuated_flag
				}
			}
			add_state_core = 664
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				NOT = { 
					45 = { 
						is_core_of = HUN 
					} 
					has_country_flag = HUN_v_evacuated_flag
				}
			}
			add_state_core = 45
		}
		
	}

		}
		HUN_substract_10_agitation = yes
	}

country_event = { # Hungary gets proposal for Antonescu Deal
	id = LH.208
	title = LH.208.t 
	desc = LH.208.d 
	picture = GFX_report_event_vienna_award_hungary
	
	is_triggered_only = no 
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = HUN 
		OR = {
			has_completed_focus = HUN_demand_transylvan_monarch
			GER = { has_completed_focus = GER_second_vienna_award }
		}
		has_full_control_of_state = 76
		NOT = { has_full_control_of_state = 84 }
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes 
	
	option = {	# Accept!
		name = LH.208.a
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = ROM
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				82 = {
					is_claimed_by = HUN
				}
			}
			remove_state_claim = 82
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				82 = {
					is_core_of = HUN
				}
			}
			82 = {
				remove_core_of = HUN
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				83 = {
					is_claimed_by = HUN
				}
			}
			remove_state_claim = 83
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				83 = {
					is_core_of = HUN
				}
			}
			83 = {
				remove_core_of = HUN
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				84 = {
					is_claimed_by = HUN
				}
			}
			remove_state_claim = 84
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				84 = {
					is_core_of = HUN
				}
			}
			84 = {
				remove_core_of = HUN
			}
		}
		76 = {
			remove_core_of = ROM
		}
		
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = ROM
			modifier = HUN_ROM_antonescu_deal
		}
		
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = ROM
			modifier = HUN_ROM_antonescu_deal
		}
		
		set_country_flag = HUN_antonescu_compromise_flag
		
	}
	
	option = {	# Decline!
		name = LH.208.b
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_political_power = 50
	}
}

country_event = {	# Romanian Terms
	id = LH.246
	title = LH.246.t 
	desc = LH.246.d 
	picture = GFX_report_event_vienna_award_hungary
	
	fire_only_once = no 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes 

	option = {	# Sign the Deal
		name = LH.246.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = HUN_transylvania_given_whole_flag
				has_global_flag = HUN_northern_transylvania_given_flag
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = HUN_transylvania_given_whole_flag
			}
			HUN = { transfer_state = 82 }
			HUN = { transfer_state = 83 }
			HUN = { transfer_state = 84 }
			HUN = { transfer_state = 76 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = HUN_territory_payments_give_1
				}
				remove_ideas = HUN_territory_payments_give_1
				add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_territory_payments_give_3 days = 365 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = HUN_territory_payments_give_2
				}
				remove_ideas = HUN_territory_payments_give_2

				has_war_with = SOV

					infantry = { x = 0 y = 3 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 3 }
				}
				support = {
					artillery = { x = 0 y = 0 }  # Spanish Arty Rgt/Bge had 2 Bn 105mm arty

			}

				remove_unit_leader = 1113
			}
		
		}
		
	
		create_corps_commander = {
			name = "Agustín Muñoz Grandes"

				division = "name = \"División de Infantería\" division_template = \"División de Infantería\" start_experience_factor = 1.0" 
				owner = HUN
			}
			create_unit = {

				owner = HUN
			}
		}

	}

# Organize the Blackshirts civil war event
country_event = {
	id = LH.259
	title = LH.259.t
	desc = LH.259.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ger_civil_war

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = ENG
		HUN = { 
			has_completed_focus = HUN_infiltrate_britain
		}
		ENG = {
			NOT = { has_government = fascism }
			has_stability < 0.5
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}

	immediate = {
		ENG = {
			hidden_effect = {
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = ENG_steady_as_she_goes 
					uncomplete_children = yes 
					refund_political_power = no 
				}
				complete_national_focus = ENG_organize_the_blackshirts
				HUN = {
					if = {
						limit = { is_in_faction = no }
						create_faction = HUN_BETHLEN_FACTION
					}
					add_to_faction = ENG
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = HUN
					value = 50
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = befriend
					id = HUN
					value = 50
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = protect
					id = HUN
					value = 50
				}
				add_stability = 30
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_owned_by = ENG
						NOT = { has_state_flag = ENG_has_blackshirt_support }
					}
					set_state_flag = ENG_has_no_blackshirt_support
				}
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						has_state_flag = ENG_has_blackshirt_support
					}
					ENG = { set_capital = { state = PREV } }
				}
				start_civil_war = {
					ruling_party = fascism
					ideology = democratic
					size = 0.5
					states = all
					states_filter = {
						has_state_flag = ENG_has_no_blackshirt_support
					}
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = fascism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = 0.51
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.05
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.15
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = ENG
						has_government = democratic
					}
					save_event_target_as = democratic_uk_civil_war
					every_unit_leader = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								has_id = 999
							}
						}
						set_nationality = ENG
					}
					ENG = {
						transfer_navy = { target = PREV }
						hidden_effect = {
							every_unit_leader = {
								limit = {
									OR = {
										has_id = 983
										has_id = 984
										has_id = 985
										has_id = 986
										has_id = 987
										has_id = 988
										has_id = 989
										has_id = 990
										has_id = 991
										has_id = 992
									}
								}
								set_nationality = event_target:democratic_uk_civil_war
							}
						}
					}
				}
				event_target:democratic_uk_civil_war = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_full_control_of_state = 126
						}
						set_capital = { state = 126 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_full_control_of_state = 132
						}
						set_capital = { state = 132 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_full_control_of_state = 128
						}
						set_capital = { state = 128 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_full_control_of_state = 127
						}
						set_capital = { state = 127 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_full_control_of_state = 132
						}
						set_capital = { state = 132 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_full_control_of_state = 130
						}
						set_capital = { state = 130 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_full_control_of_state = 121
						}
						set_capital = { state = 121 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_full_control_of_state = 133
						}
						set_capital = { state = 133 }
					}
					else = {
						random_owned_state = {
							limit = {
								is_on_continent = europe
							}
							event_target:democratic_uk_civil_war = { set_capital = { state = PREV } }
						}
					}
				}
				event_target:democratic_uk_civil_war = {
					division_template = {
						name = "Loyalist Brigade"
						priority = 1
						division_names_group = ENG_DEM_01
						is_locked = yes
						regiments = {
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
						}
					}
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							is_on_continent = europe
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "division_template = \"Loyalist Brigade\" start_experience_factor = 0 start_equipment_factor = 1"
							owner = PREV
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "division_template = \"Loyalist Brigade\" start_experience_factor = 0 start_equipment_factor = 1"
							owner = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Ok
	option = {
		name = LH.259.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_democratic_civil_war_tt
		ENG = {
			hidden_effect = {
				RAJ = { retire_country_leader = yes }
			}
			hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = mtg_news.41 days = 1 } }
			division_template = {
				name = "Blackshirt Brigade"
				priority = 1
				division_names_group = ENG_FAS_01
				is_locked = yes
				regiments = {
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_on_continent = europe
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"Blackshirt Brigade\" start_experience_factor = 0 start_equipment_factor = 1"
					owner = ROOT
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"Blackshirt Brigade\" start_experience_factor = 0 start_equipment_factor = 1"
					owner = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			unlock_national_focus = HUN_germany_trade_deal
			set_party_name = { ideology = fascism long_name = HUN_nyilas_party name = HUN_nyilas_party }
			add_ideas = HUN_empower_right_2
			country_event = { id = LH.176 days = 7 }
		}
		set_country_flag = HUN_panzerfaust_succeeded_flag
		
	}
	
	option = {	# WAR
		name = LH.272.b
		GER = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = HUN
				type = puppet_wargoal_focus
			}
			set_country_flag = GER_hun_resisted_panzerfaust_flag
		}
		set_country_flag = HUN_resisted_panzerfaust_flag
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = { remove_resource_rights = 155 }
			GER = { remove_resource_rights = 972 }
		}
	}

		}

			set_global_flag = CZE_protested_flag

			limit = { tag = ROM }
			set_global_flag = ROM_protested_flag

		}
	}

country_event = {	# Countries that protested get informed, choose to form Little Entente and attack Hungary. 
	id = LH.282
	title = LH.282.t 
	desc = LH.282.d 
	picture = GFX_report_event_hungary_refused
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {	# Form the Little Entente and attack!
		name = LH.282.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 45
			modifier = {
				strength_ratio = { tag = HUN ratio > 1.5 }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_global_flag = HUN_little_entente_3_flag
				factor = 1.5
			}
		}
		
		## Create the faction ### 
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_rule = { can_create_factions = yes }
		}
		create_faction = HUN_LITTLE_ENTENTE
		
		### Add the nations to the faction ### 
		
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = {
					tag = CZE
				}
				has_global_flag = CZE_protested_flag 
			}
			ROOT = {
				add_to_faction = CZE
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = {
					tag = ROM
				}
				has_global_flag = ROM_protested_flag 
			}
			ROOT = {
				add_to_faction = ROM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = {
					tag = YUG
				}
				has_global_flag = YUG_protested_flag 
			}
			ROOT = {
				add_to_faction = YUG
			}
		}
		
		### Declare war ###
		
		declare_war_on = {
			type = topple_government
			target = HUN
			generator = {  }
		}
		
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT 
			}
			add_to_war = { 
				targeted_alliance = PREV 
				enemy = HUN 
				hostility_reason = asked_to_join
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			HUN = {
				country_event = { id = LH.286 days = 2 }
			}
		}
		
		set_global_flag = HUN_little_entente_war_flag
		
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = LH_news.17
		}
	}
	
	option = {	# It isn't worth it.
		name = LH.282.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				HUN = {
					is_guaranteed_by = ITA
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				HUN = {
					is_guaranteed_by = BUL
				}
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		HUN = { country_event = { id = LH.285 days = 2 } }
	}

}

country_event = {	# Event for transferring Albanian territory
	id = LH.292
	title = LH.292.t 
	desc = LH.292.d 
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference
	
	is_triggered_only = no 
	
	trigger = {
		any_state = {
			has_state_flag = HUN_albanian_territory_warranted_flag
			OR = {
				is_controlled_by = HUN
				controller = {
					is_in_faction_with = HUN
					NOT = { tag = ALB }
				}
			}	
			
		}
		original_tag = HUN
		ALB = {
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = HUN
				is_in_faction = no
			}
			exists = yes
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7
	}
	
	fire_only_once = no 
	
	
	option = {	# It was the deal
		name = LH.292.a
		every_state = {
			limit = {

	title = LH.334.t 
	desc = LH.334.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hungary_parliament
	
	is_triggered_only = yes 
	
	fire_only_once = yes 
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = HUN_historical_activated_flag
	}
	
	option = { # Deny his resignation because it would cause the opposition to win
		name = LH.334.a
		set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = HUN_MEP_long name = HUN_MEP }
		add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = -0.12 }
	}
	
	option = { # give it to him CHANGE TO FASCIST TREE
		name = LH.334.b
		load_focus_tree = LH_fascist
		unlock_national_focus = HUN_empower_the_far_right
		complete_national_focus = HUN_pardon_political_extremists
		complete_national_focus = HUN_a_new_middle_class	
		
	}
}

# Imrédy's ancestral documents event for historical route!!
country_event = {
	id = LH.335
	title = LH.335.t
	desc = LH.335.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hun_burn_books
	
	is_triggered_only = no  
	
	fire_only_once = yes 
	
	trigger = {
		has_completed_focus = HUN_mem
		has_country_flag = HUN_imredy_prime_flag
		date > 1939.02.15
		NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_third_prime_minister_flag }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = HUN_third_prime_minister_flag
		hidden_effect = {
			deactivate_advisor = HUN_bela_imredy_prime
			clr_country_flag = HUN_imredy_prime_flag
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Teleki
		name = LH.335.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_teleki_was_prime_minister_flag }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_teleki_replaces_prime_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			deactivate_advisor = HUN_istvan_bethlen
		}
		activate_advisor = HUN_pal_teleki_prime
		clr_country_flag = HUN_imredy_prime_flag
		set_country_flag = HUN_teleki_prime_flag
		set_country_flag = HUN_teleki_was_prime_minister_flag
		set_country_flag = HUN_conservative_prime_minister_flag
		clr_country_flag = HUN_right_wing_prime_minister_flag
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_historical_choice_tt
		
		if = { 
			limit = { has_idea = HUN_magyar_elet }
			remove_ideas = HUN_magyar_elet
		}
			
		add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 0.15 }
	}
	
	option = { # Darányi 
		name = LH.335.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_daranyi_was_prime_minister_flag }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_daranyi_replaces_prime_tt	
		hidden_effect = {
			deactivate_advisor = HUN_kalman_daranyi
		}
		activate_advisor = HUN_kalman_daranyi_prime
		clr_country_flag = HUN_imredy_prime_flag
		set_country_flag = HUN_daranyi_prime_flag
		set_country_flag = HUN_daranyi_was_prime_minister_flag
		set_country_flag = HUN_conservative_prime_minister_flag
		clr_country_flag = HUN_right_wing_prime_minister_flag
			
		if = { 
			limit = { has_idea = HUN_magyar_elet }
			remove_ideas = HUN_magyar_elet
		}
			
		add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 0.15 }
	}
	
	option = { # Kállay 
		name = LH.335.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_kallay_was_prime_minister_flag }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_kallay_replaces_prime_tt
		hidden_effect = {	
			deactivate_advisor = HUN_miklos_kallay
		}
		activate_advisor = HUN_miklos_kallay_prime
		clr_country_flag = HUN_imredy_prime_flag
		set_country_flag = HUN_kallay_prime_flag
		set_country_flag = HUN_conservative_prime_minister_flag
		clr_country_flag = HUN_right_wing_prime_minister_flag
			
		if = { 
			limit = { has_idea = HUN_magyar_elet }
			remove_ideas = HUN_magyar_elet
		}
			
		add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 0.15 }
	}
}

		original_tag = HUN
		date > 1938.05.28
		NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_first_jew_law_enacted_flag }
		has_completed_focus = HUN_strengthen_the_regency_monarch
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	
	option = { # accept 
		name = LH.336.a

		add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.05 }
		HUN_add_10_influence_points = yes
		set_country_flag = HUN_first_jew_law_enacted_flag
	}
}

# Szálasi is released from prison after second vienna award!!
country_event = {
	id = LH.337
	title = LH.337.t
	desc = LH.337.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_purge_speech
	
	is_triggered_only = no 
	
	fire_only_once = yes 
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = HUN
		OR = {
			GER = { has_completed_focus = GER_second_vienna_award }
			HUN = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_transylvania_demanded
			}	
		}
		has_completed_focus = HUN_ban_arrow_cross
		HUN = {
			has_full_control_of_state = 76
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	
	option = { # accept 
		name = LH.337.a
		HUN_szalasi_ferenc = {
			clr_character_flag = HUN_imprisoned_flag
			set_portraits = {
				army = {
					small = "GFX_idea_HUN_szalasi_ferenc"
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = HUN_szalasi_imprisoned_flag
		add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.05 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
		show_ideas_tooltip = HUN_szalasi_ferenc
	}
}

# NSZMPHM is banned after synagoge attack during Teleki, a month later they make Nyilaskeresztes Párt
country_event = {
	id = LH.338
	title = LH.338.t 
	desc = LH.338.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ger_civil_war
	
	is_triggered_only = no 
	
	fire_only_once = yes   
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = HUN
		has_country_flag = HUN_conservative_prime_minister_flag
		date > 1939.02.01
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	
	option = { # accept 
		name = LH.338.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = nszmphm_support
				value = party_popularity@fascism
			}
			multiply_temp_variable = {
				var = nszmphm_support
				value = -0.5
			}
		}
		add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = nszmphm_support }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = LH.339 days = 20 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {	# Hungary gets the option to white peace the Little Entente
	id = LH.340
	title = LH.340.t 
	desc = LH.340.d 
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_volunteers_01
	
	is_triggered_only = no
	
	fire_only_once = yes 
	
	trigger = {
		tag = HUN
		has_war = yes 
		has_global_flag = {
			flag = HUN_little_entente_war_flag
			days > 31
		}
		surrender_progress > 0.6
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7
	}
	
	option = {	# Surrender!
		name = LH.340.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					has_war_with = ROM
				}
				has_global_flag = ROM_protested_flag
			}
			ROM = {
				country_event = { id = LH.354 hours = 3 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					has_war_with = CZE 
				}
				has_global_flag = CZE_protested_flag
			}
			CZE = {
				country_event = { id = LH.354 hours = 3 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					has_war_with = YUG 
				}
				has_global_flag = YUG_protested_flag
			}
			YUG = {
				country_event = { id = LH.354 hours = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {	# We can still win!
		name = LH.340.b
		add_war_support = 0.1
	}

}

### TRADE RELIANCE AXIS AFTER 2 YEARS
country_event = {
	id = LH.348
	title = LH.348.t
	desc = LH.348.d 
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_speech
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = no
	
	trigger = {
		has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = HUN_trade_deal_modifier }
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = HUN_ger_trade_partner_flag
				days > 730
			}
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = HUN_ita_trade_partner_flag
				days > 730
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = HUN_empower_the_far_right }
	}
	
 
	option = {# Well damn... 
		name = LH.348.a
		HUN_add_10_influence_points = yes 
		HUN_substract_10_agitation = yes 
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_government = fascism } }
			add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.1 }
		}
		#add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = HUN_economic_dependancy }
		#add_opinion_modifier = { target = ENG modifier = HUN_economic_isolation }
		#add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = HUN_economic_isolation }
		#add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = HUN_economic_isolation }
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_ger_trade_partner_flag}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = HUN_economic_dependancy }
			if = {
				limit = { GER = { has_idea = free_trade } }
				add_ideas = free_trade
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { GER = { has_idea = export_focus } }
				add_ideas = export_focus
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { GER = { has_idea = limited_exports } }
				add_ideas = limited_exports
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { GER = { has_idea = closed_economy } }
				add_ideas = closed_economy
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						is_embargoing = GER 
						is_embargoed_by = GER
					}
				}
				HUN = {
					send_embargo = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_ita_trade_partner_flag}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = ITA modifier = HUN_economic_dependancy }
			if = {
				limit = { ITA = { has_idea = free_trade } }
				add_ideas = free_trade
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ITA = { has_idea = export_focus } }
				add_ideas = export_focus
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ITA = { has_idea = limited_exports } }
				add_ideas = limited_exports
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ITA = { has_idea = closed_economy } }
				add_ideas = closed_economy
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						is_embargoing = ITA 
						is_embargoed_by = ITA
					}
				}
				HUN = {
					send_embargo = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = ENG modifier = HUN_economic_isolation }
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = HUN_economic_isolation }
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = HUN_economic_isolation }
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = HUN_economic_isolation }
		set_country_flag = HUN_trade_reliance_flag
	}
}

### TRADE RELIANCE ALLIES AFTER 2 YEARS
country_event = {
	id = LH.349
	title = LH.349.t
	desc = LH.349.d 
	picture = GFX_report_event_degaulle_churchill
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = no
	
	trigger = {
		has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = HUN_trade_deal_modifier }
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = HUN_eng_trade_partner_flag
				days > 730
			}
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = HUN_usa_trade_partner_flag
				days > 730
			}
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = HUN_fra_trade_partner_flag
				days > 730
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = HUN_utilize_the_march_front }
	}
	
 
	option = {# Well damn... 
		name = LH.349.a
		HUN_substract_10_influence_points = yes 
		HUN_add_10_agitation = yes 
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_government = democratic } }
			add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.1 }
		}
		#add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = HUN_economic_dependancy }
		#add_opinion_modifier = { target = ENG modifier = HUN_economic_isolation }
		#add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = HUN_economic_isolation }
		#add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = HUN_economic_isolation }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_eng_trade_partner_flag}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = ENG modifier = HUN_economic_dependancy }
			if = {
				limit = { ENG = { has_idea = free_trade } }
				add_ideas = free_trade
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ENG = { has_idea = export_focus } }
				add_ideas = export_focus
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ENG = { has_idea = limited_exports } }
				add_ideas = limited_exports
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ENG = { has_idea = closed_economy } }
				add_ideas = closed_economy
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						is_embargoing = ENG 
						is_embargoed_by = ENG
					}
				}
				HUN = {
					send_embargo = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_fra_trade_partner_flag}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = HUN_economic_dependancy }
			if = {
				limit = { FRA = { has_idea = free_trade } }
				add_ideas = free_trade
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { FRA = { has_idea = export_focus } }
				add_ideas = export_focus
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { FRA = { has_idea = limited_exports } }
				add_ideas = limited_exports
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { FRA = { has_idea = closed_economy } }
				add_ideas = closed_economy
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						is_embargoing = FRA 
						is_embargoed_by = FRA
					}
				}
				HUN = {
					send_embargo = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_usa_trade_partner_flag}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = HUN_economic_dependancy }
			if = {
				limit = { USA = { has_idea = free_trade } }
				add_ideas = free_trade
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { USA = { has_idea = export_focus } }
				add_ideas = export_focus
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { USA = { has_idea = limited_exports } }
				add_ideas = limited_exports
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { USA = { has_idea = closed_economy } }
				add_ideas = closed_economy
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						is_embargoing = USA 
						is_embargoed_by = USA
					}
				}
				HUN = {
					send_embargo = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = HUN_economic_isolation }
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = ITA modifier = HUN_economic_isolation }
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = HUN_economic_isolation }
		set_country_flag = HUN_trade_reliance_flag
	}
}


### TRADE RELIANCE COMINTERN AFTER 2 YEARS
country_event = {
	id = LH.350
	title = LH.350.t
	desc = LH.350.d 
	picture = GFX_report_event_SOV_demands
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = no
	
	trigger = {
		has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = HUN_trade_deal_modifier }

			flag = HUN_sov_trade_partner_flag
			days > 730
		}
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = HUN_council_of_commisars }
	}
	
 
	option = {# Well damn... 
		name = LH.350.a
		HUN_substract_10_influence_points = yes 
		HUN_add_10_agitation = yes

			limit = { NOT = { has_government = communism } }
			add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = 0.1 }
		}
		#add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = HUN_economic_dependancy }
		#add_opinion_modifier = { target = ENG modifier = HUN_economic_isolation }
		#add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = HUN_economic_isolation }
		#add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = HUN_economic_isolation }

			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_sov_trade_partner_flag}

			}
			else_if = {

	desc = LH.351.d 
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_defensive_preparations
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = no 
	
	trigger = {
		tag = HUN
		has_war_with_major = yes
		has_civil_war = no
	}
 
	option = {# Well damn... 
		name = LH.351.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = HUN_treaty_of_triannon_aat }
			remove_ideas = HUN_treaty_of_triannon_aat
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = HUN_treaty_of_triannon }
			remove_ideas = HUN_treaty_of_triannon
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = HUN_treaty_of_triannon_2 }
			remove_ideas = HUN_treaty_of_triannon_2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = HUN_treaty_of_triannon_3 }
			remove_ideas = HUN_treaty_of_triannon_3
		}
	}
	
}

country_event = {	# Imre Nagy/Rákosi Takes Over / Revolution or peaceful takover?
	id = LH.405
	title = LH.405.t
	desc = {
		text = LH.405.nagy.d
		trigger = {	
			OR = {
				power_balance_value = {
					id = HUN_kadar_bad_tree_bop
					value < -0.85
				}
				power_balance_value = {
					id = HUN_rakosi_tree_bop
					value < -0.85
				}
			}
			#NOT = {
				# Quadrumvirate has high power!
			#}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = LH.405.rakosi.d
		trigger = {	
			# Quadrumvirate has high power!
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_hun_nagy_speech
	
	fire_only_once = yes 
	
	is_triggered_only = no 

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			power_balance_value = {
				id = HUN_kadar_bad_tree_bop
				value < -0.85
			}
			power_balance_value = {
				id = HUN_rakosi_tree_bop
				value < -0.85
			}
			# Quadrumvirate has high power!
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 7 }

	option = {# Revolution!
		name = LH.405.a
		### Civil war!
	}
	
	option = {# Peaceful takeover
		name = LH.405.b
		if = {	### Imre Nagy Takover
			limit = { 
				OR = {
					power_balance_value = {
						id = HUN_kadar_bad_tree_bop
						value < -0.85
					}
					power_balance_value = {
						id = HUN_rakosi_tree_bop
						value < -0.85
					}
					#NOT = { # Quadrumvirate has high power! }
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic 
				elections_allowed = yes 			
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = HUN_NAGY
			uncomplete_national_focus = {
				focus = HUN_new_leadership 
				uncomplete_children = yes 
				refund_political_power = no 
			}
			set_popularities = {
				democratic = 43
				communism = 42
				fascism = 5
				neutrality = 10
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = SOV }
				SOV = {
					remove_from_faction = HUN
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_puppet_of = SOV }
				SOV = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = HUN
						autonomy_state = autonomy_free
						end_wars = no
						end_civil_wars = no
					}
				}
			}
			
			unlock_national_focus = HUN_organize_an_official_party
			set_country_flag = HUN_imre_nagy_overthrew_government_flag
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				# Quadrumvirate has high power!
			}
			### Rákosi takes over
		}
	}
	
}

	id = LH.424
	title = LH.424.t
	desc = LH.424.d 
	picture = GFX_report_event_gre_cabinet_meeting
	
	fire_only_once = no 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes 
	
	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_negyesfogat_kadar_flag }
			country_event = { id = LH.424 hours = 24 }
		}
		set_variable = { quadrumvirate_influence_gain = modifier@HUN_quad_increase_daily }
		add_to_variable = {
			var = quadrumvirate_influence
			value = quadrumvirate_influence_gain
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = quadrumvirate_influence
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
	}

	option = {# 
		name = LH.424.a
		
	}
}

country_event = {	# hidden event that gives Germany a puppet wargoal if agitation is high enough
	id = LH.425
	title = LH.425.t
	desc = LH.425.d 
	picture = GFX_report_event_gre_cabinet_meeting
	
	fire_only_once = no 
	
	is_triggered_only = no  
	
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		AND = {
			GER = { check_variable = { var = ger_agitation_value value = 0.80 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
			GER = { check_variable = { var = ger_agitation_value value = 1 compare = less_than } }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				HUN = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
			}
			GER = {
				remove_from_faction = HUN
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				AND = {
					GER = { check_variable = { var = ger_agitation_value value = 0.90 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
					GER = { check_variable = { var = ger_agitation_value value = 1 compare = less_than } }
				}
			}
			GER = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = puppet_wargoal_focus
					target = HUN
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}

	option = {# 
		name = LH.425.a
		
	}
}

#END of Economic Crisis Event
country_event = {
	id = LH.475
	title = LH.475.t
	desc = LH.475.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hun_gyori_program
	
	is_triggered_only = no 
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = HUN_economic_crisis_1 }
		### CONSUMER GOODS
		check_variable = {
			var = HUN_crisis_consumer_goods_factor 
			value = 0
			compare = equals
		}
		### CONSTRUCTION SPEED
		check_variable = {
			var = HUN_crisis_production_speed_buildings_factor
			value = 0
			compare = equals
		}
		### FACTORY OUTPUT 
		check_variable = {
			var = HUN_crisis_industrial_capacity_factory
			value = 0
			compare = equals
		} 
		NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_special_factory_construction_flag }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}

	option = {# N
		name = LH.475.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_remove_crisis_tt
		hidden_effect = { remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = HUN_economic_crisis_1 } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = HUN_refuse_to_pay_debts
			}
			set_variable = { HUN_good_crisis_consumer_goods_factor = 0 }
			set_variable = { HUN_good_crisis_industrial_capacity_factory = 0 }
			set_variable = { HUN_good_crisis_production_lack_of_resource_penalty_factor = 0 }
			set_variable = { HUN_good_crisis_production_lack_of_resource_penalty_factor = 0 }
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = HUN_economic_crisis_3 }
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = HUN_economic_crisis_2 }
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = HUN_economic_crisis_1 }
			}
			HUN_reset_trade_deal_modifier = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_get_hungarian_economy_tt
			hidden_effect = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = HUN_economic_crisis_good } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = HUN_refuse_to_pay_debts }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_get_hungarian_economy_tt
			hidden_effect = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = HUN_economic_crisis_good } }
			subtract_from_variable = { var = HUN_good_crisis_production_lack_of_resource_penalty_factor value = 0.08 }
			clr_country_flag = HUN_economic_crisis_1_flag
			set_country_flag = HUN_economic_crisis_good_flag
		}
	}
	
	
}

	id = LHelections.1
	title = LHelections.1.t 
	desc = LHelections.1.d 
	picture = GFX_report_event_hungary_parliament
	
	is_triggered_only = yes 

	fire_only_once = yes 
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1 
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = HUN_daranyi_crisis_flag
			set_country_flag = HUN_second_prime_minister_flag
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			if = { 
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_daranyi_prime_flag }
				deactivate_advisor = HUN_kalman_daranyi_prime
				clr_country_flag = HUN_daranyi_prime_flag
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_bethlen_prime_flag }
				deactivate_advisor = HUN_istvan_bethlen_prime
				clr_country_flag = HUN_bethlen_prime_flag
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_szell_prime_flag }
				deactivate_advisor = HUN_jozsef_szell
				clr_country_flag = HUN_szell_prime_flag
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {	# Imrédy 
		name = LHelections.1.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_imredy_was_prime_minister_flag }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_imredy_replaces_prime_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = conservative_prime_minister_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_historical_choice_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			deactivate_advisor = HUN_bela_imredy
		}
		activate_advisor = HUN_bela_imredy_prime
		hidden_effect = { 
			remove_trait = {
				character = HUN_bela_imredy_prime
				slot = political_advisor
				trait = prime_minister_imredy
			}
			add_trait = {
				character = HUN_bela_imredy_prime
				slot = political_advisor
				trait = prime_minister_imredy_historical
			}
		}
			clr_country_flag = HUN_daranyi_prime_flag
			clr_country_flag = HUN_bethlen_prime_flag
			clr_country_flag = HUN_szell_prime_flag
			set_country_flag = HUN_imredy_prime_flag
			set_country_flag = HUN_imredy_was_prime_minister_flag
			set_country_flag = HUN_imredy_replaced_daranyi_flag
		
	}
	option = {	# choose Bárdossy
		name = LHelections.1.b 
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_bardossy_was_prime_minister_flag }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_bardossy_replaces_prime_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = conservative_prime_minister_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			deactivate_advisor = HUN_laszlo_bardossy
		}
		activate_advisor = HUN_laszlo_bardossy_prime
		clr_country_flag = HUN_daranyi_prime_flag
		clr_country_flag = HUN_bethlen_prime_flag
		clr_country_flag = HUN_szell_prime_flag

		set_country_flag = HUN_bardossy_was_prime_minister_flag

		}

		}

country_event = {	# hidden event that checks popularities
	id = LHelections.23
	title = LHelections.23.t 
	desc = LHelections.23.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote
	
	fire_only_once = yes 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	hidden = yes
	
	immediate = {
	
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = n_pop
			value = party_popularity@neutrality
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = f_pop
			value = party_popularity@fascism
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = c_pop
			value = party_popularity@communism
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = d_pop
			value = party_popularity@democratic
		}
		
		add_to_temp_variable = {
			var = c_pop
			value = d_pop
		}
		
		add_to_temp_variable = {
			var = n_pop
			value = f_pop
		}
		
		if = {	# NO SUCCESS
			limit = { check_variable = { var = n_pop value = c_pop compare = greater_than } }
			country_event = LHelections.25
		}
		else_if = {	# SUCCESS
			limit = { check_variable = { var = c_pop value = n_pop compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
			country_event = LHelections.24
		}
	}
	
	
	option = {	# Oh well
		name = LHelections.23.a
		
	}

}

country_event = {	# Rákosi takes over!
	id = LHelections.26
	title = LHelections.26.t 
	desc = {
		text = LHelections.26.election.d 
		trigger = {	
			has_country_flag = HUN_elections_failed_flag
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = LHelections.26.bop.d 
		trigger = {	
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_elections_failed_flag }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_ITA_italian_civil_war
	
	fire_only_once = yes 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {	# Oh well
		name = LHelections.26.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_elections_failed_flag }
			clr_country_flag = HUN_elections_failed_flag
			hidden_effect = {
				set_capital = { state = 43 }
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = communism 
				ideology = ROOT 
				size = 0.4
				capital = 973
				states = {
					973 155
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = 45
				}
				#load_focus_tree = LH_monarchy
				set_cosmetic_tag = HUN_RAKOSI
			}
			
			unlock_national_focus = HUN_new_leadership
			uncomplete_national_focus = { focus = HUN_organize_an_official_party uncomplete_children = yes refund_political_power = no }
			#set_politics = { ruling_party = communism }
			promote_character = HUN_matyas_rakosi
			set_party_name = { ideology = communism long_name = HUN_MDP_long name = HUN_MDP }
			clr_country_flag = HUN_kadar_leader_flag 
			hidden_effect = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = HUN_RAKOSI
				set_country_flag = HUN_rakosi_leader_flag
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_elections_failed_flag } }
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_power_balance = {
						id = HUN_communism_bop
					}
				}
				remove_power_balance = {
					id = HUN_communism_bop
				}
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = communism 
				ideology = neutrality 
				size = 0.7
				capital = 154
				states = {
					154 972 43
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = HUN_RAKOSI
				add_stability = 0.4
				add_war_support = 0.6
			}
		}
		
	}

}

		set_country_flag = HUN_rakosi_cooldown_flag
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 0.2 }
		}
	}

}

country_event = {	# Solve the Monarchy Question fascism
	id = LHelections.30
	title = LHelections.30.t 
	desc = {
		text = LHelections.30.no_boszormeny.d
		trigger = {	
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_boszormeny_prime_flag
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = LHelections.30.boszormeny.d
		trigger = {	
			has_country_flag = HUN_boszormeny_prime_flag
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_royal_parade
	
	fire_only_once = yes 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes 
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = HUN_proclaim_szlasi_the_leader_of_the_nation_fascism }
				country_event = { id = LH.305 days = 40 }	### MAGYARFÖLD EVENT
			}
		}
	}
	
	
	option = {	# Crown Friedrich Franz
		name = LHelections.30.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_boszormeny_prime_flag }
		}
		set_country_flag = HUN_friedrich_fascist_king_flag
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = "HUN_franz_friedrich"
			country_leader = {
			  ideology=nazism
			  expire="1965.1.1"
			}
			promote_leader = yes
		}
		remove_ideas = HUN_monarchy_without_monarch
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = LH_news.39 days = 2 }
			country_event = { id = LHelections.31 days = 60 }
		}
		GER = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = befriend
				id = HUN
				value = 100
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = protect
				id = HUN
				value = 100
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { modifier = HUN_german_king target = HUN }
		}
	}

	option = {	# Crown Albrecht Habsburg-Teschen
		name = LHelections.30.b
		every_country = {
			limit = { is_neighbor_of = HUN }
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { modifier = HUN_habsburg_king target = PREV }
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_boszormeny_prime_flag }
		}
		set_country_flag = HUN_albrecht_fascist_king_flag
		promote_character = {
			character = HUN_albrecht_habsburg
			ideology = gen_nazism
		}
		remove_ideas = HUN_monarchy_without_monarch
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = LH_news.39 days = 2 }
			country_event = { id = LHelections.31 days = 60 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {	# Abolish the Monarchy once and for all
		name = LHelections.30.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_boszormeny_prime_flag }
		}
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_pm_takes_over_tt
		country_event = { id = LH.176 days = 7 }	### Event for inauguration without king
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = HUN_side_with_the_workers
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_historical_choice_tt
		}
	}

	option = {	# Böszörmény is crowned king
		name = LHelections.30.d
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = HUN_boszormeny_prime_flag
		}
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		set_cosmetic_tag = HUN_KKP
		remove_ideas = HUN_monarchy_without_monarch
	}

}
